(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});

At this point, the sauce should coat the pasta but still be loose enough to pool around the edges of the pan. Add butter, and stir and toss rapidly to melt and emulsify into the sauce. Remove from heat, add 3/4 of grated cheese and all of the parsley, and stir rapidly to incorporate. Season with salt to taste. Serve immediately, passing remaining grated cheese at the table."
} ]

<div id="heading_1-0" class="comp heading heading--updated-article-header"> <h1 class="heading__title">Pasta ai Funghi (Creamy Pasta With Mushrooms)</h1>
<p class="heading__subtitle">Shallots, garlic, white wine, and Parmesan bring out the earthy flavors of mushrooms in this comforting all-weather pasta.</p>
</div>
<div id="article-meta_container_1-0" class="comp article-meta_container mntl-block"><div id="article-meta_1-0" class="comp article-meta mntl-block article-meta--updated-article-header" data-tracking-container="true"><div id="lifestyle-food-bylines_1-0" class="comp lifestyle-food-bylines mntl-bylines"><div id="mntl-bylines__group_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__group mntl-block mntl-bylines__group--author"><div id="mntl-bylines__item_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__item mntl-attribution__item mntl-attribution__item--has-date">

<div data-tooltip="Sasha is a senior culinary editor at Serious Eats. <div id="article__header--project_1-0" class="comp article__header--project mntl-sc-page mntl-block article-intro text-passage structured-content" data-sc-sticky-offset="200" data-sc-ad-label-height="11" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="1" data-sc-content-positions="[1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true"><div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-callout mntl-sc-block-callout mntl-block theme-whyitworks text-passage" data-tracking-id="mntl-sc-block-callout" data-tracking-container="true"><h3 id="mntl-sc-block-callout-heading_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-heading mntl-text-block">Why It Works</h3>
<div id="mntl-sc-block-callout-body_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-body mntl-text-block text-passage"><ul><li>Adding gelatin to chicken stock gives the final sauce a glossy, pasta-coating finish.</li><li>A splash of fish sauce gives fresh mushrooms a subtle savory boost.</li><li>Fresh parsley balances the earthy richness of the dish.</li></ul></div></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_2-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Even though mushrooms are generally equated with the cool months of autumn, there are plenty of wild mushrooms that hit their seasonal peaks at other times of the year. Plus, modern cultivation methods have made a variety of fresh &#39;shrooms available year-round, which is great news for those of us who love cooking and eating them all the time.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_3-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_4-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> For this rich and hearty pasta ai funghi, we brown a mix of fresh mushrooms in a hot skillet and then cook them down into an earthy sauce with aromatics, white wine, and gelatin-enriched chicken stock. Many mushroom pasta and risotto recipes call for expensive dried porcini mushrooms—and there&#39;s no arguing that they pack a ton of savory flavor in a small package—but you can make delicious versions of both dishes without them. Here, we use a (very non-traditional) splash of fish sauce to give the mushrooms a savory boost. Finishing the sauce with butter and Parmesan cheese gives it a creamy richness, and a handful of chopped fresh parsley leaves offer a pop of brightness.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_5-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_6-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> You can decide whether to pair the sauce with dried pasta or delicate, fresh egg-dough noodles. Either way, this comforting cool-weather dish is perfect for a cozy evening at home any time of the year.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_7-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_8-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-callout mntl-sc-block-callout mntl-block theme-originalpublishdate text-passage" data-tracking-id="mntl-sc-block-callout" data-tracking-container="true"><h3 id="mntl-sc-block-callout-heading_2-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-heading mntl-text-block">April 2020</h3></div></div>
<div id="structured-project-content_1-0" class="comp structured-project-content mntl-block article__content right-rail structured-content"><div id="recipe-decision-block_1-0" class="comp recipe-decision-block"> <p class="recipe-decision-block__header">Recipe Details</p>

<section id="section--ingredients_1-0" class="comp section--ingredients section"> <header class="section__header "><div class="loc section-header"><div id="mntl-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-block section-header--ingredients"><h2 id="text-block_1-0" class="comp text-block section__title"> Ingredients </h2></div> </div></header>
<div class="loc section-content section__content "><div id="structured-ingredients_1-0" class="comp structured-ingredients">
<ul class="structured-ingredients__list text-passage">
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">240</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ml</span>) <a href="https://www.seriouseats.com/pressure-cooker-chicken-stock-recipe" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">homemade</a> or store-bought <span data-ingredient-name="true">low-sodium chicken stock</span> (see note)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1 1/2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoons</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) powdered <span data-ingredient-name="true">gelatin</span>, such as Knox</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">tablespoons</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">30</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ml</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">extra-virgin olive oil</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1 1/2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">pounds</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">675</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) mixed <span data-ingredient-name="true">mushrooms</span> (such as <span data-ingredient-name="true">shiitake</span>, <span data-ingredient-name="true">oyster</span>, <span data-ingredient-name="true">maitake, beech</span>, <span data-ingredient-name="true">cremini</span>, and <span data-ingredient-name="true">chanterelles</span>), cleaned, trimmed, and thinly sliced or torn by hand (see note)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-name="true">Kosher salt</span> and freshly <span data-ingredient-name="true">ground black pepper</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">3</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">medium</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">shallots</span>, finely minced (about <span data-ingredient-quantity="true">3/4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span>; <span data-ingredient-quantity="true">120</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">medium</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">10</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">garlic cloves</span>, minced</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">tablespoons</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) chopped <span data-ingredient-name="true">fresh thyme leaves</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1/2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">120</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ml</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">dry white wine</span> or <span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1/4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">60</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ml</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">dry sherry</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoon</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">5</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ml</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">fish sauce</span> (optional)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">pound</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">450</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) <span data-ingredient-name="true">short dried pasta</span> (such as <span data-ingredient-name="true">casarecce</span> or <span data-ingredient-name="true">gemelli</span>) or <span data-ingredient-name="true">long </span><a href="https://www.seriouseats.com/fresh-egg-pasta" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1"><span data-ingredient-name="true">fresh egg-dough pasta</span></a> (such as <span data-ingredient-name="true">tagliatelle</span> or <span data-ingredient-name="true">fettuccine</span>)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">6</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">tablespoons</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">unsalted butter</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">3</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ounces</span>; <span data-ingredient-quantity="true">85</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">3</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">ounces</span> grated <span data-ingredient-name="true">Parmigiano-Reggiano</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span>; <span data-ingredient-quantity="true">85</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>)</p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1/4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> (<span data-ingredient-quantity="true">10</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">g</span>) chopped <span data-ingredient-name="true">fresh flat-leaf parsley leaves</span></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

<section id="section--instructions_1-0" class="comp section--instructions section"> <header class="section__header "><h2 class="section__title " data-title-tag="">Directions</h2></header>
<div class="loc section-content section__content "><div id="structured-project__steps_1-0" class="comp structured-project__steps mntl-sc-page mntl-block text-passage structured-content" data-sc-sticky-offset="60" data-sc-ad-label-height="24" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="1" data-sc-content-positions="[300,600,900,1200,1500,1800,2100]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true"><OL id="mntl-sc-block_9-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--OL">
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_10-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_11-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Pour stock into a small bowl or liquid measuring cup and evenly sprinkle gelatin over surface of stock. Set aside.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_12-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_14-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_15-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> In a large 12-inch cast iron or stainless steel skillet, heat oil over medium-high heat until shimmering. Add mushrooms, season with salt and pepper, and cook, stirring frequently with a wooden spoon, until moisture has evaporated and mushrooms are deeply browned, 12 to 15 minutes.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_16-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_18-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_19-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Add shallots, garlic, and thyme and cook, stirring constantly, until fragrant and shallots are softened, 30 seconds to 1 minute. Add wine or sherry, and cook, swirling pan and scraping up any stuck-on bits with a wooden spoon, until wine is reduced by half, about 30 seconds.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_20-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_22-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_23-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Add chicken stock mixture, season lightly with salt, and bring to a simmer. Reduce heat to medium-low, add fish sauce (if using), and cook, stirring occasionally, until mushroom mixture is thickened to a saucy consistency, about 5 minutes. Turn off heat.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_24-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_26-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_27-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Meanwhile, in a pot of salted boiling water, cook pasta. If using dry pasta, cook until just shy of al dente (1 to 2 minutes less than the package directs). If using fresh pasta, cook until noodles are barely cooked through. Using either a spider skimmer (for short pasta) or tongs (for long fresh pasta), transfer pasta to pan with mushrooms along with 3/4 cup (180ml) pasta cooking water. Alternatively, drain pasta using a colander or fine-mesh strainer, making sure to reserve at least 2 cups (475ml) pasta cooking water.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_28-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_30-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_31-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Heat sauce and pasta over high and cook, stirring and tossing rapidly, until pasta is al dente (fresh pasta will never be truly al dente) and sauce is thickened and coats noodles, 1 to 2 minutes, adding more pasta cooking water in 1/4 cup (60ml) increments as needed. At this point, the sauce should coat the pasta but still be loose enough to pool around the edges of the pan. Add butter, and stir and toss rapidly to melt and emulsify into the sauce. Remove from heat, add 3/4 of grated cheese and all of the parsley, and stir rapidly to incorporate. Season with salt to taste. Serve immediately, passing remaining grated cheese at the table.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_32-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
</OL>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-special-equipment"></span><h2 id="mntl-sc-block_35-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> Special Equipment </span> </h2>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_36-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Large <a href="https://www.seriouseats.com/best-cast-iron-skillet" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">cast iron</a> or <a href="https://www.seriouseats.com/best-stainless-steel-skillets" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">stainless steel skillet</a>, <a href="https://www.seriouseats.com/best-spider-spoon-8600888" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="3">spider skimmer</a>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_37-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-notes"></span><h2 id="mntl-sc-block_38-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> Notes </span> </h2>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_39-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Remove the stems of hard-stemmed mushrooms, like shiitakes, before using; tender-stemmed mushrooms, like oyster, can be used with the stem on. Firmer mushrooms like shiitakes are best sliced, whereas more tender mushrooms can be easily torn into bite-size pieces by hand.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_40-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-make-ahead-and-storage"></span><h2 id="mntl-sc-block_41-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> Make-Ahead and Storage </span> </h2>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_42-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> This pasta is at its best when enjoyed immediately, especially when made with fresh pasta. If using dried pasta, it does keep well for leftovers, however, and can be refrigerated in an airtight container for up to 3 days.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_43-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>

<span class="card__title">
<span class="card__underline">
Fast and Easy Pasta With Blistered Cherry Tomato Sauce Recipe
</span>
</span>
<div id="card__author-name_1-0" class="comp card__author-name mntl-block" data-byline-author="By J. Kenji López-Alt"></div> </div>
</div>
</a></div>
<div id="card-list__item_2-0" class="comp card-list__item mntl-block"><a id="card_2-0" class="comp card" href="https://www.seriouseats.com/jamie-olivers-summer-tagliatelle-with-parsley-recipe">
<div class="loc card__header"><div class="card__media mntl-image universal-image__container">
<img
data-src="https://www.seriouseats.com/thmb/Kv4P2dXO6hQPnAedHYbN4o-gwX8=/375x250/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/__opt__aboutcom__coeus__resources__content_migration__serious_eats__seriouseats.com__recipes__images__2012__05__20120530-dt-jamie-olivers-summer-parsley-pasta-b66f033af1594040b2c86bb5bb7a866c.jpg"

const brandId = '55631c8a-65ef-454b-9544-3e8e173a3af3';

const lightboxJs = digiohFastActivation === 'true' ? '/lightbox_speed.js' : '/lightbox_inline.js';

this.script = script;
this.initialized = true;
},
load(callback) {
this.init();

Mntl.utilities.loadExternalJS({ src: this.script }, callback);
} else {
Mntl.utilities.loadExternalJS({ src: this.script });
}
}
